# Wine Appellations

**Source:** [https://developer.commerce7.com/docs/wine-appellations](https://developer.commerce7.com/docs/wine-appellations)

**Section:** resources

---
Appellations are a property available on wine products. Commerce7 has a standard list of appellations to choose from. Below is a sample response, but we are continually adding new appellations to the system. Please check to see if your appellation exists in Commerce7's standard list. If it doesn't, reach out to [[email protected]](/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#0d7e787d7d627f794d6e626060687f6e683a236e6260).
* * *
# 
List appellations
**`GET`** `/wine-appellation`
**Response**  
An array of `wineAppellations` and total count
JSON
